[28/02/25, 4:28:46â€¯PM] Anthony-Agent-Friendly Realtors: BRH Agent: *Power of Attorney (PoA) Process for Property Sale*
Step 1: Adhere to the "Law of the Land" (local regulations). Have a lawyer in Bangalore (India) draft the PoA and send a soft copy to the owner. Ensure the owner signs every page.
Step 2: In the U.S., the PoA must be" stamped" at the Indian Embassy and couriered to Bangalore/Your Address.
Step 3: Submit the PoA for "adjudication" at the District Registrarâ€™s Office (DRO) in Bangalore. Once adjudicated, you will have a legally valid PoA to execute the Sale Deed.

*Important:* PoA is only valid between immediate family members such as parents, siblings, spouse, and children (direct blood relations). It does not apply to extended family like cousins, aunts, or uncles.

1) *TIMINGS FOR POSTINGS*
Strictly between 8.00 AM to 9.00 PM. 

2) *WHAT TO POST*
Only messages related to Real Estate availability and requirements.

 *NO GOOD MORNING/ GOOD NIGHT POSTS AT ALL. NO POSITIVE THOUGHTS / FUN / MOCKERY POSTS/ MESSAGES.* 
 
3) *PHOTOS*
 *Maximum of 2 photos related to Real Estate inventory.* 

4) *VIDEOS*
 Please post link to the videos & not the video itself.

No photos / videos of Developer Projects as a backdrop or in the interest of promoting their projects as a whole.

*5) CONGRATULATORY MESSAGES*
Please send Congratulatory messages to other members only on their private windows. Letâ€™s keep the groups confined to inventory & requirements only.

Members are requested to strictly follow the above guidelines and *VIOLATION* of any guideline will invite  Group Admins to take suitable action.
